3. 2*x + x*dy/dx + y + 2*y*dy/dx + 5 = 0
4. Rearrange: make dy/dx
5. (x + 2*y)*dy/dx + 2*x + y + 5 = 0
6. Answer: dy/dx = (-2*x - y - 5)/(x + 2*y)
